Values: dashboard|downloads|purchases|profile|subscriptions|licenses. Default: \"dashboard\"\n- `showSupport` (boolean): Toggle support link visibility. Default: true\n- `supportUrl` (string): URL to support portal/helpdesk. Default: empty\n- `supportLabel` (string): Support link text. Default: \"My Tickets\"\n\n#### Editor UI (edit.js)\n- **InspectorControls:**\n  - SelectControl for defaultTab (dashboard, downloads, purchases, profile)\n  - ToggleControl for showSupport\n  - TextControl for supportUrl (type=\"url\")\n  - TextControl for supportLabel\n- **Editor Preview:** Shows mockup with user icon, description, and pill-style tab preview\n\n#### Frontend Render (render.php)\n- **Guard:** Requires `class_exists('Easy_Digital_Downloads')`\n- **Authentication:** Shows login form with redirect if not logged in\n- **Tab Navigation:** Built dynamically via switch statement calling:\n  - `wbcom_essential_edd_render_dashboard_tab($customer)`\n  - `wbcom_essential_edd_render_subscriptions_tab($customer)`\n  - `wbcom_essential_edd_render_downloads_tab($customer)`\n  - `wbcom_essential_edd_render_licenses_tab($customer)`\n  - `wbcom_essential_edd_render_purchases_tab($customer)`\n  - `wbcom_essential_edd_render_profile_tab()`\n\n- **REST API Endpoint:** `POST wbcom/v1/edd-account/{tab}`\n  - Route: `/plugins/gutenberg/blocks/edd-account-dashboard/edd-account-dashboard.php` line 40\n  - Callback: `wbcom_essential_edd_account_tab_callback()`\n  - Requires: `is_user_logged_in()`\n  - Nonce: wp_rest\n  - Validates tab parameter against whitelist\n\n- **Tab Detection:** \n  - Query param `?tab=` → $active_tab\n  - Fallback to block attribute defaultTab\n  - Valid tabs: dashboard, subscriptions, downloads, licenses, purchases, profile\n\n- **Conditional Tabs:**\n  - Subscriptions: Only if `class_exists('EDD_Recurring')`\n  - Licenses: Only if `function_exists('edd_software_licensing')`\n\n- **Dashboard Tab Content:**\n  - User greeting with first_name fallback to display_name\n  - Stats cards: Total Orders, Total Spent, Active Licenses (if SL), Active Subscriptions (if Recurring)\n  - Recent orders table (3 latest, status: complete or partially_refunded)\n  - EDD Functions used:\n    - `edd_get_customer_by('user_id', $user->ID)`\n    - `edd_currency_filter()`\n    - `edd_format_amount()`\n    - `edd_software_licensing()->licenses_db->get_licenses()`\n    - `EDD_Subscriptions_DB->get_subscriptions()`\n    - `edd_get_orders()`\n    - `edd_date_i18n()`\n    - `edd_display_amount()`\n    - `edd_get_status_label()`\n\n- **Subscriptions Tab Content:**\n  - `EDD_Subscriptions_DB->get_subscriptions()` with customer_id filter\n  - Shows: product name, plan name (via `edd_get_price_option_name()`), status, amount/period, start date, next renewal, countdown urgency, times billed\n  - Upgrade links via `edd_sl_get_license_upgrades()`\n  - Cancel URL with nonce `edd-recurring-cancel`\n  - Urgency indicator: days_left ≤ 7 (critical), ≤ 30 (warning)\n\n- **Downloads Tab Content:**\n  - `edd_get_orders()` with customer_id, status=[complete,partially_refunded]\n  - Groups items by product\n  - File list with download links\n\n- **Purchases Tab:**\n  - Order history table with number, date, amount, status\n\n- **Profile Tab:**\n  - `[edd_profile_editor]` shortcode\n\n- **Sidebar Navigation:**\n  - Links have data-tab attribute for AJAX switching\n  - Active tab indicated by is-active class and aria-current=\"page\"\n  - Support link has target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\"\n  - Logout link via `wp_logout_url()`\n\n#### Frontend Interactivity (view.js)\n- **Tab Switching:** AJAX via fetch() using REST API endpoint\n- **Cache:** Client-side cache for loaded tab content\n- **History API:** window.history.pushState() for URL updates\n- **Form Action Fix:** Rewrites form actions to current page URL with ?tab= parameter\n- **Interactions:**\n  - License key copy-to-clipboard with Clipboard API fallback\n  - Confirmation dialog for subscription cancellation (data-confirm attribute)\n- **Loading State:** Opacity overlay with spinner (aria-busy)\n\n#### CSS Patterns (style.scss)\n- **BEM Naming:** `.wbcom-edd-account__*`\n- **CSS Variables:**\n  - `--edd-sidebar-width: 240px`\n  - `--edd-sidebar-bg: #f8fafc`\n  - `--edd-nav-active-color: var(--wbcom-link-color, #2563eb)`\n  - `--edd-nav-active-bg: #eff6ff`\n  - `--edd-nav-indicator-width: 3px`\n  - Font scale variables: xs(12px), sm(13px), base(14px), md(15px), lg(17px), xl(22px), 2xl(28px)\n- **Layout:** Flexbox sidebar + content (sticky sidebar)\n- **States:** `.is-active` for active nav links, `.is-copied` for copy button feedback\n- **Responsive:** Wide/full alignment removes border-radius and side borders\n- **Interactive Elements:** Hover states, focus-visible outlines, smooth transitions (0.18s)\n\n#### EDD Integration Points\n- Requires EDD class to exist\n- Uses EDD Customer, Order, Subscription, Download, License APIs\n- Integrates with EDD Recurring and Software Licensing add-ons conditionally\n- Calls EDD shortcodes: `[edd_profile_editor]`, `[edd_receipt]`\n- REST endpoint validates against EDD tab whitelist\n\n---\n\n### 2. EDD ENHANCED CHECKOUT\n**Location:** `/plugins/gutenberg/blocks/edd-checkout-enhanced/`\n\n#### Block Configuration (block.json)\n```\nname: wbcom-essential/edd-checkout-enhanced\nversion: 1.0.0\ncategory: starter-design\nicon: cart\nsupports: align=[wide,full], spacing={margin,padding}\n```\n\n#### Attributes\n- `showProgressBar` (boolean): Display 4-step progress indicator. Default: true\n- `showTrustBadges` (boolean): Show security/trust badges below checkout. Default: true\n- `trustBadgeText` (string): Main badge text. Default: \"Secure checkout powered by Stripe\"\n- `showReviews` (boolean): Display customer reviews. Default: true\n- `reviewCount` (number): Reviews to show (1-6). Default: 3\n- `showRecommendations` (boolean): Show product recommendations. Default: true\n- `recommendationCount` (number): Recommendations to show (1-6). Default: 3\n\n#### Editor UI (edit.js)\n- **InspectorControls:**\n  - PanelBody \"Checkout Options\":\n    - ToggleControl: showProgressBar\n    - ToggleControl: showTrustBadges\n    - TextControl: trustBadgeText (conditional on showTrustBadges)\n  - PanelBody \"Social Proof\":\n    - ToggleControl: showReviews\n    - RangeControl: reviewCount (1-6, conditional on showReviews)\n  - PanelBody \"Recommendations\":\n    - ToggleControl: showRecommendations\n    - RangeControl: recommendationCount (1-6, conditional on showRecommendations)\n- **Editor Preview:** Cart icon, description, and conditional badges\n\n#### Frontend Render (render.php)\n- **Guard:** Requires `class_exists('Easy_Digital_Downloads')`\n- **Structure:** [Progress Bar] → [Checkout Form] → [Trust Badges] → [Reviews] → [Recommendations]\n\n- **Progress Bar** (if enabled):\n  - 4 steps: Cart (completed) → Details (active) → Payment (upcoming) → Complete (upcoming)\n  - Step connectors with filled state\n  - Checkmark for completed steps\n\n- **Checkout Form:**\n  - Renders `[download_checkout]` shortcode\n\n- **Trust Badges** (if enabled):\n  - 3 badges shown:\n    1. Shield icon: Trust badge text (customizable)\n    2. Checkmark icon: \"14-Day Money Back\"\n    3. Chat icon: \"Priority Support\"\n  - Payment method icons: Visa, Mastercard, PayPal, Stripe\n  - Uses SVG inline icons\n\n- **Reviews Section** (if enabled):\n  - Gets reviews from EDD Reviews add-on\n  - Queries cart products first, fallback to all reviews\n  - `get_comments()` with type='edd_review', status='approve'\n  - Star rating calculation (aggregate and per-review)\n  - Review grid with: title, text (trimmed to 25 words), author, product, rating\n  - Meta: average rating, review count\n\n- **Recommendations Section** (if enabled):\n  - Requires `function_exists('edd_rp_get_multi_suggestions')`\n  - Calls `edd_rp_get_multi_suggestions($cart_ids, $user_id, $recommendation_count)`\n  - Shows: product thumbnail, name, rating, price, \"Add to Cart\" button\n  - Rating calculated from EDD Reviews meta\n\n- **EDD Functions Used:**\n  - `edd_get_cart_contents()`\n  - `get_comments()` with edd_review type\n  - `get_comment_meta()` for 'edd_rating', 'edd_review_title'\n  - `edd_rp_get_multi_suggestions()`\n  - `edd_get_download()`\n  - `edd_price()`\n  - `edd_get_purchase_link()` for add-to-cart buttons\n\n#### CSS Patterns (style.scss)\n- **BEM Naming:** `.wbcom-edd-checkout__*`\n- **Font Scale:** xs(12px) through 2xl(28px)\n- **Progress Bar:**\n  - Grid-based step layout\n  - Connector lines with filled/empty states\n  - Step circle states: completed (blue bg), active (white bg + shadow), upcoming (gray)\n  - Smooth transitions on state change\n- **Trust Badges:** Flex layout with icon + text content\n- **Review Cards:** Grid layout with star ratings, text ellipsis\n- **Recommendation Cards:** Product cards with thumbnail, rating, price, button\n\n#### EDD Integration Points\n- Requires EDD class to exist\n- Renders EDD checkout shortcode\n- Depends on EDD Reviews add-on (optional)\n- Depends on EDD Recommendations Plus (optional)\n- Uses cart data to show contextual reviews and recommendations\n\n---\n\n### 3. EDD ORDER SUCCESS\n**Location:** `/plugins/gutenberg/blocks/edd-order-success/`\n\n#### Block Configuration (block.json)\n```\nname: wbcom-essential/edd-order-success\nversion: 1.0.0\ncategory: starter-woocommerce (NOTE: should be starter-design)\nicon: yes-alt\nsupports: align=[wide,full], spacing={margin,padding}\n```\n\n#### Attributes\n- `showSuccessHeader` (boolean): Display animated checkmark + message. Default: true\n- `accountPageUrl` (string): URL to account/downloads page. categories in grid with images, post counts, hover effects\n\n---\n\n## REGISTRATION PATTERNS\n\nAll EDD-specific blocks register conditionally:\n```php\nif ( ! class_exists( 'Easy_Digital_Downloads' ) ) {\n    return;\n}\nregister_block_type( $build_path );\nadd_action( 'init', $callback );\n```\n\nWooCommerce blocks register conditionally:\n```php\nif ( ! class_exists( 'WooCommerce' ) ) {\n    return;\n}\n```\n\nCategory Grid registers unconditionally (WordPress core).\n\n---\n\n## REST API ENDPOINTS\n\n**Only EDD Account Dashboard uses custom REST endpoints:**\n\n- **Route:** `wbcom/v1/edd-account/{tab}`\n- **Callback:** `wbcom_essential_edd_account_tab_callback()`\n- **Methods:** GET\n- **Permission:** `is_user_logged_in()`\n- **Parameter Validation:** Whitelist [dashboard, subscriptions, downloads, licenses, purchases, profile]\n- **Response:** `{ html: wp_kses_post( $content ) }`\n- **Security:** \n  - Nonce validation via X-WP-Nonce header\n  - Referer validation (host matching)\n  - REQUEST_URI override to prevent REST URL in forms\n  - Output sanitized via wp_kses_post()\n\n---\n\n## SHARED UTILITIES\n\nAll EDD account tabs use helper functions:\n- `wbcom_essential_edd_tab_header($title, $description)` — Section header\n- `wbcom_essential_edd_render_*_tab($customer)` — Individual tab renderers\n- Helper renders output via ob_start/ob_get_clean\n\n---\n\n## DEPENDENCIES & ADD-ONS CHECKED\n\n- **EDD Recurring:** Conditionally shows subscriptions tab\n- **EDD Software Licensing:** Conditionally shows licenses tab\n- **EDD Reviews:** Conditionally shows customer reviews in checkout\n- **EDD Recommendations Plus:** Conditionally shows recommendations in checkout\n- **WooCommerce:** Required for Mini Cart and Product Grid blocks\n- **WordPress Core:** Required for Category Grid block\n\n---\n\n## SECURITY OBSERVATIONS\n\n✅ **Strong Practices:**\n- All EDD output sanitized via wp_kses_post(), esc_html(), esc_url()\n- REST endpoint requires authentication check\n- Nonce validation on tab switching\n- Whitelist validation for tab parameters\n- Referer host validation prevents cross-origin exploitation\n- No unsanitized output in JavaScript (marked with eslint-disable for intentional cases)\n\n⚠ **Considerations:**\n- Product recommendations and reviews query large result sets (up to 100 reviews)\n- No pagination on subscription/download lists (hardcoded limits)\n- Cache is client-side only (could benefit from server-side caching)\n\n---\n\n## FILE LOCATIONS SUMMARY\n\n**3 Core EDD Blocks:**\n1.
